# Research Log

Daily research notes from `/pre-market` and `/weekly-prep`. Every entry is source-attributed so weekly review can measure research-source impact on trade outcomes.

---

## Format

```
## YYYY-MM-DD ‚ÄĒ /pre-market (or /weekly-prep)

**Research source:** perplexity | websearch_fallback | alpha_vantage_only | DEGRADED
**Market direction pull:** <Confirmed Uptrend | Under Pressure | Correction>
**Sector leaders (top 3):** Technology, Energy, Financials (or as applicable)
**Sector laggards (bottom 3):** REITs, Utilities, Consumer Staples

### Overnight catalysts affecting watchlist

- $NVDA: earnings beat after-hours, +3.2% AH ‚ÄĒ watch for gap-up entry
- $CRWD: analyst upgrade pre-market, within 2% of pivot

### Buy-zone status (open watchlist items)

- $ANET: pivot $112.50, last $111.80 ‚ÄĒ within 1% of pivot, ready
- $SMCI: pivot $42.00, last $39.20 ‚ÄĒ below pivot, watching
- $PANW: earnings 3 days out ‚ÄĒ remove from buy list per 5-day rule

### Open positions ‚ÄĒ overnight check

- $NVDA (entry $487.50): last $495.00 ‚ÄĒ above entry, stop $453.38 holding
- $META (entry $621.00): flat overnight, no catalysts

### New candidates flagged

- $APP (AppLovin): positive catalyst, will run canslim-screener scoring during /market-check

### Risks

- FOMC meeting tomorrow ‚ÄĒ no new entries before 1pm CT Wed
- CPI data at 7:30 AM CT Thu ‚ÄĒ reduce new-entry willingness
```

### ‚ö†ÔłŹ CRITICAL DATA CORRECTION ‚ÄĒ AVGO

Prior pre-market (Jun 4) estimated AVGO at "+6.03% AH ‚Üí $505‚Äď510 Jun 4 open." **WRONG.**

**Actual AVGO timeline:**
- Jun 3 session close: $477.01
- Jun 3 AH: Initial pop +6.03% to ~$506 (headline beat) ‚Üí earnings call detail caused violent REVERSAL
- Sell reason: Management did NOT raise 2027 AI revenue guidance (prior guide: "in excess of $100B"). Street had priced in an upgrade. Software division slight miss.
- Jun 3 AH final: ~‚ąí14% from $477 close ‚Üí ~$410‚Äď415
- Jun 4 intraday range: $405.51 low ‚Äď $496.02 high (violent, mean-reverting session)
- Jun 4 close: est. ~$413‚Äď420 (NOT $505‚Äď510 as previously logged)
- Jun 5 pre-market: **$413.45** (confirmed via multiple sources: Yahoo Finance, Robinhood, CNBC)

**AVGO Q2 FY2026 actual results (released Jun 3 AH):**
- Revenue: $22.19B (+48% YoY) vs $22.11B est ‚Üí BEAT (minor)

- MISS: 2027 AI revenue guidance NOT raised (remained "in excess of $100B") ‚ÄĒ market catalyst for sell-off
- Stock reaction: ‚ąí14% AH ‚Üí thesis intact but market punished for "not enough"

**AVGO watchlist status CORRECTION:** Not 77‚Äď82/100 high-priority entry. Score reset pending Jun 9 re-score with:

- Base DESTROYED: needs 3‚Äď4 weeks minimum from ~$405‚Äď415 support zone

### Key finding (validates preflight design)

The pipeline correctly **rejected** a stock that *looks* like a breakout winner (NVDA at new 52w high with stellar fundamentals) because the **volume surge test failed (-14.6% below avg when +40% is required)** and **no valid base pattern** formed. Human intuition on this setup would likely be "buy" ‚ÄĒ the system correctly said "no." Fundstrat's analyst independently flagged false-breakout risk in the Perplexity research.
